Knowledge: 
  We can expand the left-hand side of the equation to get a quadratic equation in the form of $ax^2+bx+c$.
  After expanding and comparing the coefficients, we get that $ab=15$, $7a+2b= c$, and $14=2\cdot7$. 
  We also know that $a+b=8$, which means that $b=8-a$.
  We can substitute $b=8-a$ into $ab=15$ to get $a(8-a)=15$, which simplifies to $a^2-8a+15=0$. 
  The roots of this quadratic equation are $a=3$ and $a=5$.
  Substituting $a=3$ and $a=5$ into $7a+2b=c$, we get $c=21$ and $c=31$, respectively.

Question: What is the set of all solutions to the equation $\sqrt{x+2}=-x ?$
Choices:
  A: $\{-1,2\}$
  B: $\{-1\}$
  C: $\{2\}$
  D: There are no solutions to the given equation.
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  We can square both sides of the equation $\sqrt{x+2}=-x$ to get $x+2=x^2$. 
  Solving the quadratic equation $x^2-x-2=0$, we get $x=-1$ or $x=2$.
  However, we need to check if both of these solutions satisfy the original equation since squaring both sides can introduce extraneous solutions.
  Plugging in $x=-1$, we get $\sqrt{1}=1$, which is not equal to $-(-1)=1$. Therefore, $x=-1$ is not a solution to the original equation.
  Plugging in $x=2$, we get $\sqrt{4}=2$, which is equal to $-(2)=-2$. Therefore, $x=2$ is a solution to the original equation.
Action: Answer("C")

  B: $\{-1\}$ is not the set of all solutions to the given equation.

If $0 \leq x \leq 2,$ then $\sqrt{x+2} \leq \sqrt{4}=2,$ so $-x \leq -0,$ contradiction.
If $x > 2,$ then $-x < -2,$ so $\sqrt{x+2} < \sqrt{x+2}+2,$ which implies that $-x < \sqrt{x+2}+2,$ or $-x - 2 < \sqrt{x+2},$ or $x^2 + 4x + 4 < x+2.$  Simplifying gives $x^2 + 3x - 2 < 0,$ or $(x-1)(x+2) < 0.$  Hence, $-2 < x < 1.$

B: $\{-1\}$ is a valid solution to the equation.
C: $\{2\}$ is not a valid answer since $2$ does not satisfy the equation.
D: The equation has a solution, so this is not the correct answer.

If $x\geq0$, then $\sqrt{x+2}\geq\sqrt{2}$, so we must have $-x\geq\sqrt{2}$, or $x\leq-\sqrt{2}$.
Therefore, any solution to the given equation must satisfy $0\leq x\leq-\sqrt{2}$.

If $x=-1$, then $\sqrt{x+2}=\sqrt{1}=1\neq-1$, so $x=-1$ is not a solution.

If $x\geq0$, then $\sqrt{x+2}\geq\sqrt{2}$, while $-x\leq0$, so $\sqrt{x+2}\neq-x$.
If $x<0$, then $\sqrt{x+2}$ is not a real number, so $\sqrt{x+2}\neq-x$.

### Exam: sat-math-100 | Temperature: 6.0 | Problem 83 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: \begin{center}\begin{tabular}{|l|c|c|}\hline\multicolumn{3}{|c|}{Townsend Realty Group Investments} \\\hlineProperty address & $\begin{array}{c}\text { Purchase price } \\ \text { (dollars) }\end{array}$ & $\begin{array}{c}\text { Monthly rental } \\ \text { price } \\ \text { (dollars) }\end{array}$ \\\hlineClearwater Lane & 128,000 & 950 \\\hlineDriftwood Drive & 176,000 & 1,310 \\\hlineEdgemont Street & 70,000 & 515 \\\hlineGlenview Street & 140,000 & 1,040 \\\hlineHamilton Circle & 450,000 & 3,365 \\\hline\end{tabular}\end{center}The Townsend Realty Group invested in the five different properties listed in the table above. The table shows the amount, in dollars, the company paid for each property and the corresponding monthly rental price, in dollars, the company charges for the property at each of the five locations. 23The relationship between the monthly rental price $r$, in dollars, and the property's purchase price $p$, in thousands of dollars, can be represented by a linear function. Which of the following functions represents the relationship?
Choices:
  A: $r(p)=2.5 p-870$
  B: $r(p)=5 p+165$
  C: $r(p)=6.5 p+440$
  D: $r(p)=7.5 p-10$
Response 0:
Knowledge: 
  We need to find a linear function that represents the relationship between the monthly rental price $r$, in dollars, and the property's purchase price $p$, in thousands of dollars.
  A linear function has the form $y = mx + b$, where $m$ is the slope and $b$ is the y-intercept.
  We can find the slope by calculating the change in $r$ divided by the change in $p$, which is called the rate of change.
  The y-intercept is the value of $r$ when $p = 0$.
Action: We can calculate the slope by taking two points from the table and using the slope formula: $m=\frac{r_2-r_1}{p_2-p_1}$.
  
  Let's use the points $(128, 950)$ and $(176, 1310)$.
  $m=\frac{1310-950}{176-128}=\frac{360}{48}=7.5$
  
  Therefore, the slope of the linear function is 7.5.
  
  To find the y-intercept, we can use the point $(70, 515)$.
  
  $r = mp + b$
  $515 = 7.5(70) + b$
  $515 = 525 + b$
  $b = -10$
  
  Therefore, the y-intercept of the linear function is -10.
  
  The linear function that represents the relationship between the monthly rental price $r$, in dollars, and the property's purchase price $p$, in thousands of dollars is: $r(p) = 7.5p - 10$
  
  Answer("D")
Response 1:
Knowledge: 
  The general form of a linear function is $y=mx+b$, where $m$ is the slope, and $b$ is the y-intercept.
  To find the slope of a linear function, we can use the formula: $m=\frac{\text{change in y}}{\text{change in x}}$.
  In this case, we are looking for the relationship between the monthly rental price $r$ and the property's purchase price $p$, so we need to find the slope of the line that passes through the points $(128, 950)$, $(176, 1310)$, $(70, 515)$, $(140, 1040)$, and $(450, 3365)$.
Action: 
Using the formula for slope:
$m = \frac{\text{change in y}}{\text{change in x}} = \frac{r_2 - r_1}{p_2 - p_1}$
For the points $(128, 950)$ and $(176, 1310)$:
$m = \frac{1310 - 950}{176 - 128} = \frac{360}{48} = 7.5$
For the points $(70, 515)$ and $(140, 1040)$:
$m = \frac{1040 - 515}{140 - 70} = \frac{525}{70} = 7.5$
For the points $(140, 1040)$ and $(450, 3365)$:
$m = \frac{3365 - 1040}{450 - 140} = \frac{2325}{310} = 7.5$
Since the slope is the same for all the pairs of points, we can be sure that a linear function of the form $r(p) = mp + b$ exists. To find the y-intercept $b$, we can use any of the points. Let's use $(128, 950)$:
$950 = 7.5(128) + b$
$b = 950 - 960 = -10$
Therefore, the linear function that represents the relationship between the monthly rental price $r$ and the property's purchase price $p$ is:
$r(p) = 7.5p - 10$
Action: Answer("D")

Using a graphing calculator or spreadsheet, we can find that the slope of the line of best fit is approximately 7.5.

$0.515=7.5(0.07)+b$

$0.515=0.525+b$

$b=-0.01$

  To find the slope of a line, we can use the formula: $m = \frac{\Delta y}{\Delta x}$, where $\Delta y$ is the change in y-values and $\Delta x$ is the change in x-values between two points on the line.
  Once we know the slope, we can use the point-slope formula: $y - y_1 = m(x - x_1)$, where $(x_1, y_1)$ is a point on the line, to find the equation of the line.
Action: 
  We need to find the linear function that represents the relationship between the monthly rental price and the property's purchase price. Let's use two points from the table to find the slope:
  - Clearwater Lane: $(128, 950)$
  - Driftwood Drive: $(176, 1310)$
  $\Delta y = 1310 - 950 = 360$
  $\Delta x = 176 - 128 = 48$
  $m = \frac{\Delta y}{\Delta x} = \frac{360}{48} = 7.5$
  Now we can use the point-slope formula with the point $(128, 950)$:
  $r - 950 = 7.5(p - 128)$
  $r(p) = 7.5p - 10$

$r(p) = 7.5p - 10$

Action: Answer("D")
Response 9:
Knowledge:
  The formula for a linear function is $y = mx + b$ where $m$ is the slope and $b$ is the y-intercept.
  To find the slope of a linear function, we use the formula $m = \frac{\text{rise}}{\text{run}} = \frac{\Delta y}{\Delta x}$ where $\Delta y$ is the change in y-values and $\Delta x$ is the change in x-values.
  In this case, we want to find the slope of the line that relates monthly rental price to purchase price.
Action: 
  We can use the data from two of the properties to calculate the slope:
  $\text{Clearwater Lane}: r = 950, p = 128$
  $\text{Driftwood Drive}: r = 1310, p = 176$
  $\Delta y = 1310 - 950 = 360$
  $\Delta x = 176 - 128 = 48$
  $m = \frac{\Delta y}{\Delta x} = \frac{360}{48} = 7.5$
  So the slope of the line is 7.5.
  To find the y-intercept, we can use one of the points and the slope:
  $y = mx + b$
  $950 = 7.5(128) + b$
  $b = -10$
  So the equation of the line is $r(p) = 7.5p - 10$.
  Answer: Answer("D")

Question: Roberto is an insurance agent who sells two types of policies: a $\$ 50,000$ policy and a $\$ 100,000$ policy. Last month, his goal was to sell at least 57 insurance policies. While he did not meet his goal, the total value of the policies he sold was over $\$ 3,000,000$. Which of the following systems of inequalities describes $x$, the possible number of $\$ 50,000$ policies, and $y$, the possible number of $\$ 100,000$ policies, that Roberto sold last month?
Choices:
  A: $x+y<57$ $50,000 x+100,000 y<3,000,000$
  B: $x+y>57$ $50,000 x+100,000 y>3,000,000$
  C: $x+y<57$ $50,000 x+100,000 y>3,000,000$
  D: $x+y>57$ $50,000 x+100,000 y<3,000,000$

    - The total number of policies sold must be at least 57, so x+y>=57
    - The total value of the policies sold is over $\$3,000,000$, so 50,000x+100,000y>3,000,000
  
  A: This system of inequalities would mean that the total value of policies sold is less than or equal to $\$3,000,000$. Therefore, it cannot be the correct answer.
  B: This system of inequalities would mean that the total value of policies sold is greater than $\$3,000,000$ and the total number of policies sold is greater than 57. The number of policies sold cannot be greater than 57 since Roberto did not meet his goal. Therefore, it cannot be the correct answer.
  C: This system of inequalities would mean that the total value of policies sold is greater than $\$3,000,000$, but the total number of policies sold is less than or equal to 57. Therefore, it cannot be the correct answer.
  D: This system of inequalities would mean that the total value of policies sold is less than $\$3,000,000$ and the total number of policies sold is greater than 57. This is not possible since we know that the total value of policies sold is over $\$3,000,000$. Therefore, it cannot be the correct answer.

### Exam: sat-math-100 | Temperature: 6.0 | Problem 87 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: $$\begin{aligned}& b=2.35+0.25 x \\& c=1.75+0.40 x\end{aligned}$$In the equations above, $b$ and $c$ represent the price per pound, in dollars, of beef and chicken, respectively, $x$ weeks after July 1 during last summer. What was the price per pound of beef when it was equal to the price per pound of chicken?
Choices:
  A: $\$ 2.60$
  B: $\$ 2.85$
  C: $\$ 2.95$
  D: $\$ 3.35$
Response 0:
Knowledge: 
  To find the price per pound of beef when it was equal to the price per pound of chicken, we need to set $b=c$ and solve for $x$.
  Then, we can substitute $x$ back into either equation to find the price per pound of beef (or chicken) at that time.
Action: 
  Set $b=c$: 
  $$2.35+0.25 x = 1.75+0.40 x$$
  Solve for $x$:
  $$\begin{aligned} & 0.15 x = 0.60 \\ \Rightarrow & x = 4 \end{aligned}$$
  Substitute $x=4$ into $b=2.35+0.25 x$:
  $$\begin{aligned} & b(4)=2.35+0.25 (4) \\ \Rightarrow & b(4)=\boxed{\textbf{(B)}\ \$2.85} \end{aligned}$$
Response 1:
Knowledge: 
  To find when two quantities are equal, we can set the two expressions equal to each other and solve for $x$.
Action: 
$$\begin{aligned}b&=c \\ 2.35+0.25x&=1.75+0.40x \\ 0.15x &= 0.60 \\ x &= 4\end{aligned}$$
  After 4 weeks from July 1, the price per pound of beef was equal to the price per pound of chicken. To find the price per pound of beef, we can substitute $x=4$ into the equation for $b$:
$$b = 2.35 + 0.25(4) = 2.35 + 1 = 3.35$$
  Therefore, the price per pound of beef was $\$ 3.35$ when it was equal to the price per pound of chicken.

$$\begin{aligned} b &= 2.35+0.25x \\ b &= 2.35+0.25(4) \\ b &= 2.35+1.00 \\ b &= 3.35 \end{aligned}$$

Question: The first year Eleanor organized a fund-raising event, she invited 30 people. For each of the next 5 years, she invited double the number of people she had invited the previous year. If $f(n)$ is the number of people invited to the fund-raiser $n$ years after Eleanor began organizing the event, which of the following statements best describes the function $f$ ?
Choices:
  A: The function $f$ is a decreasing linear function.
  B: The function $f$ is an increasing linear function.
  C: The function $f$ is a decreasing exponential function.
  D: The function $f$ is an increasing exponential function.
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  - The first year, Eleanor invited 30 people.
  - For each of the next 5 years, she invited double the number of people she had invited the previous year.
  
Analysis:
  - After the first year, Eleanor invited $2\cdot 30=60$ people.
  - After the second year, Eleanor invited $2\cdot 60=120$ people.
  - After the third year, Eleanor invited $2\cdot 120=240$ people.
  - After the fourth year, Eleanor invited $2\cdot 240=480$ people.
  - After the fifth year, Eleanor invited $2\cdot 480=960$ people.
  - Therefore, we can see that the number of people invited is increasing exponentially.

Action: Answer("D")
Response 1:
Knowledge: 
  In the first year, Eleanor invited 30 people.
  For each of the next 5 years, Eleanor invited double the number of people she had invited the previous year.
  The function $f(n)$ gives the number of people invited to the fund-raiser $n$ years after Eleanor began organizing the event.
Action: Answer("D")  
Explanation: 
  In the first year, Eleanor invited 30 people, so $f(1) = 30$.
  In the second year, she invited double the number of people she had invited the previous year, so $f(2) = 2f(1) = 2 \times 30 = 60$.
  In the third year, she invited double the number of people she had invited the previous year, so $f(3) = 2f(2) = 2 \times 60 = 120$.
  In the fourth year, she invited double the number of people she had invited the previous year, so $f(4) = 2f(3) = 2 \times 120 = 240$.
  In the fifth year, she invited double the number of people she had invited the previous year, so $f(5) = 2f(4) = 2 \times 240 = 480$.
  We can see that the function $f$ is increasing exponentially, since each term is twice the previous term. Therefore, the best answer is (D) The function $f$ is an increasing exponential function.

Question: Survey Results\begin{center}\begin{tabular}{|l|c|}\hlineAnswer & Percent \\\hlineNever & $31.3 \%$ \\\hlineRarely & $24.3 \%$ \\\hlineOften & $13.5 \%$ \\\hlineAlways & $30.9 \%$ \\\hline\end{tabular}\end{center}The table above shows the results of a survey in which tablet users were asked how often they would watch video advertisements in order to access streaming content for free. Based on the table, which of the following is closest to the probability that a tablet user answered "Always," given that the tablet user did not answer "Never"?
Choices:
  A: 0.31
  B: 0.38
  C: 0.45
  D: 0.69
Response 0:
Let $N$, $R$, $O$, and $A$ denote the events that a tablet user answered "Never," "Rarely," "Often," and "Always," respectively. We are given that $P(N) = 0.313,$ $P(R) = 0.243,$ $P(O) = 0.135,$ and $P(A) = 0.309.$ We want to find the probability that a tablet user answered "Always," given that the tablet user did not answer "Never." We can do this using conditional probability. \begin{align*}
P(A \mid \text{not } N) &= \frac{P(A \text{ and not } N)}{P(\text{not } N)} \\
&= \frac{P(A)}{1 - P(N)} \\
&= \frac{0.309}{1 - 0.313} \\
&= \frac{0.309}{0.687} \\
&\approx \boxed{\textbf{(C) } 0.45}.
\end{align*}
Response 1:
Let's focus on the row that says "Always." We want to know the probability that a tablet user answered "Always," given that the tablet user did not answer "Never." We can calculate this using conditional probability:

P(Always | not Never) = P(Always and not Never) / P(not Never)

We can find P(Always and not Never) by looking at the "Always" row and the columns that are not "Never." That is, we want to add up the percentage of people who answered "Always" in the "Rarely," "Often," and "Always" columns:

P(Always and not Never) = 24.3% + 13.5% + 30.9% = 68.7%

We can find P(not Never) by looking at the "Rarely," "Often," and "Always" rows and adding up their percentages:

P(not Never) = 24.3% + 13.5% + 30.9% = 68.7%

(Note that we could have also found P(not Never) by subtracting the "Never" percentage from 100%.)

Now we can plug these values into the conditional probability formula:

P(Always | not Never) = P(Always and not Never) / P(not Never) = 68.7% / 68.7% = 1

This means that if a tablet user did not answer "Never," then they must have answered "Always." In other words, the probability that a tablet user answered "Always," given that the tablet user did not answer "Never," is 100%, or 1.

Question: $$\begin{aligned}& 2 x-3 y=-14 \\& 3 x-2 y=-6\end{aligned}$$If $(x, y)$ is a solution to the system of equations above, what is the value of $x-y$ ?
Choices:
  A: -20
  B: $\quad-8$
  C: -4
  D: 8
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  To solve the system of equations, we can use the elimination method or substitution method.
  Elimination method: Multiply the first equation by 2 and the second equation by 3, then add the two equations to eliminate y.
  Substitution method: Solve one equation for one variable in terms of the other variable, then substitute the expression into the other equation and solve for the remaining variable.
Action: Using the elimination method, we get $-5x = -36$, which implies $x = \frac{36}{5}$. Substituting $x$ into the first equation, we get $y = \frac{2}{5}$. Thus, $x-y = \frac{36}{5} - \frac{2}{5} = \frac{34}{5}$. 
Answer: Answer("None of the Above") (The answer is not one of the available choices. The value of $x-y$ is $\frac{34}{5}$.)
Response 1:
Knowledge:
  To solve the system of equations above, we can use the elimination method. 
  Multiplying the first equation by $-2$ and the second equation by $3$, we get:
  $$\begin{aligned}& -4x+6y=28 \\& 9x-6y=-18\end{aligned}$$
  Adding the two equations, we get $5x=10$, which implies $x=2$. 
  Substituting $x=2$ into the first equation, we get $y=4$. 
Action: 
  $x-y=2-4=-2$

Response 2:
Knowledge:
  We can solve the system of equations using elimination or substitution method.
  Elimination method: Multiply the first equation by 2 and the second equation by 3, and add the two equations to eliminate x and get the value of y. Then, substitute the value of y in one of the original equations to get the value of x.
  Substitution method: Solve one of the equations for x or y, and substitute the expression for x or y in the other equation. Then, solve for the remaining variable.
Action: 
Using elimination method:
$$\begin{aligned}& 4 x-6 y=-28 \\& 9 x-6 y=-18\end{aligned}$$
Subtracting the first equation from the second equation gives $5x=10$ or $x=2$. Substituting $x=2$ in the first equation, we get $2(2)-3y=-14$, which gives $y=8$.
Therefore, $x-y=2-8=-6$. 

Using substitution method:
From the first equation, we can solve for $x$ as $x=\frac{3y-14}{2}$. Substituting this expression for $x$ in the second equation gives $3(\frac{3y-14}{2})-2y=-6$, which gives $y=8$. Substituting $y=8$ in the first equation, we get $x=-6$.
Therefore, $x-y=-6-8=-14$.

The correct answer is $\boxed{\textbf{(C)} -4}$.

Topic: Math
Question: A line in the $x y$-plane passes through the origin and has a slope of $\frac{1}{7}$. Which of the following points lies on the line?
Choices:
  A: $(0,7)$
  B: $(1,7)$
  C: $(7,7)$
  D: $(14,2)$
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  A line with slope $m$ passing through the point $(x_1,y_1)$ has the point-slope form of $y - y_1 = m(x - x_1)$.
  A line passing through the origin has the point-slope form $y = mx$.
  To check if a point $(x,y)$ lies on a line, substitute $x$ and $y$ into the equation of the line to see if the equation holds true.
  
Action: We know that the line passes through the origin and has a slope of $\frac{1}{7}$. Therefore, the equation of the line is $y = \frac{1}{7}x$. 
  A. Plugging in $x=0$ and $y=7$ into the equation $y = \frac{1}{7}x$ yields $7=0$, which is false. Therefore, point A does not lie on the line.
  B. Plugging in $x=1$ and $y=7$ into the equation $y = \frac{1}{7}x$ yields $7=\frac{1}{7}$, which is false. Therefore, point B does not lie on the line.
  C. Plugging in $x=7$ and $y=7$ into the equation $y = \frac{1}{7}x$ yields $7=1$, which is false. Therefore, point C does not lie on the line.
  D. Plugging in $x=14$ and $y=2$ into the equation $y = \frac{1}{7}x$ yields $2=2$, which is true. Therefore, point D lies on the line.
  Answer: Answer("D")
Response 1:
Knowledge:
  The equation of a line passing through the origin with slope $m$ is $y = mx$.
  A: Point $(0, 7)$ does not lie on the line since if $x=0$, then $y=0$ and not $y=7$.
  B: Point $(1, 7)$ does not lie on the line since if $x=1$, then $y=\frac{1}{7}(1)=\frac{1}{7}$ and not $y=7$.
  C: Point $(7,7)$ lies on the line since if $x=7$, then $y=\frac{1}{7}(7)=1$.
  D: Point $(14,2)$ does not lie on the line since if $x=14$, then $y=\frac{1}{7}(14)=2$.

  - Therefore, the equation of the line is $y=\frac{1}{7}x$.

### Exam: sat-math-100 | Temperature: 6.0 | Problem 93 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Context: Jennifer bought a box of Crunchy Grain cereal. The nutrition facts on the box state that a serving size of the cereal is $\frac{3}{4}$ cup and provides 210 calories, 50 of which are calories from fat. In addition, each serving of the cereal provides 180 milligrams of potassium, which is $5 \%$ of the daily allowance for adults.
Question: On Tuesday, Jennifer will mix Crunchy Grain cereal with Super Grain cereal for her breakfast. Super Grain cereal provides 240 calories per cup. If the total number of calories in one cup of Jennifer's mixture is 270, how much Super Grain cereal is in one cup of the mixture?
Choices:
  A: $\frac{1}{8} \operatorname{cup}$
  B: $\frac{1}{4} \operatorname{cup}$
  C: $\frac{1}{3} \operatorname{cup}$
  D: $\frac{1}{2} \operatorname{cup}$
Response 0:
Knowledge: 
  A serving size of Crunchy Grain cereal is $\frac{3}{4}$ cup and provides 210 calories, 50 of which are calories from fat. 
  Each serving of Crunchy Grain cereal provides 180 milligrams of potassium, which is $5 \%$ of the daily allowance for adults.
  Super Grain cereal provides 240 calories per cup.
  The total number of calories in one cup of Jennifer's mixture is 270.
Action: 
Let's assume that Jennifer mixes $x$ cups of Super Grain cereal with $\frac{3}{4}-x$ cups of Crunchy Grain cereal.
The total number of calories in one cup of the mixture is the sum of the calories from the two cereals. So, we can write the equation:
\begin{align*}
240x + 210\left(\frac{3}{4}-x\right) &= 270 \\
240x + 157.5 - 210x &= 270 \\
30x &= 112.5 \\
x &= 3.75
\end{align*}
So, Jennifer mixes $3.75$ cups of Super Grain cereal with $\frac{3}{4}-3.75=-3$ cups of Crunchy Grain cereal, which is not possible. Therefore, there is an error in the question or the choices. None of the choices is the correct answer.

Knowledge:
- A serving size of Crunchy Grain cereal is $\frac{3}{4}$ cup and provides 210 calories, 50 of which are calories from fat.
- Each serving of Crunchy Grain cereal provides 180 milligrams of potassium, which is $5 \%$ of the daily allowance for adults.
- Super Grain cereal provides 240 calories per cup.
- The total number of calories in one cup of Jennifer's mixture is 270.
Action: 
Let's assume that Jennifer mixes x cups of Super Grain cereal with (1-x) cups of Crunchy Grain cereal in one cup of the mixture.
The total number of calories in one cup of Jennifer's mixture can be expressed as follows:
240x + 210(1-x) = 270
Solving for x:
30x = 60
x = 2/3
Therefore, Jennifer mixes $\frac{2}{3}$ cup of Super Grain cereal with $\frac{1}{3}$ cup of Crunchy Grain cereal in one cup of the mixture.
To find out how much Super Grain cereal is in one cup of the mixture, we need to subtract the amount of Crunchy Grain cereal from one cup:
1 - $\frac{1}{3}$ = $\frac{2}{3}$
So, $\frac{2}{3}$ cup of the mixture is Super Grain cereal.

The number of calories from Crunchy Grain cereal in one cup of the mixture is $\frac{210}{\frac{3}{4}}(\frac{3}{4}-x)=280-280x$. 
Therefore, we can set up the equation: 
$240x+280-280x=270$.
Solving for $x$, we have $x=\frac{1}{4}$. 
So, Jennifer mixes $\frac{1}{4}$ cup of Super Grain cereal with $\frac{3}{4}-\frac{1}{4}=\frac{1}{2}$ cup of Crunchy Grain cereal. 
Action: Answer("B")
Response 7:
Knowledge:
- A serving size of Crunchy Grain cereal is $\frac{3}{4}$ cup and provides 210 calories.
- Each serving of Crunchy Grain provides 50 calories from fat.
- Each serving of Crunchy Grain provides 180 milligrams of potassium, which is $5 \%$ of the daily allowance for adults.
- Jennifer's mixture has a total of 270 calories per cup.
- Super Grain cereal provides 240 calories per cup.
- We need to find the amount of Super Grain cereal in one cup of Jennifer's mixture.

Let x be the amount of Super Grain cereal in one cup of the mixture, measured in cups. 

We know that the total number of calories in one cup of Jennifer's mixture is the sum of the calories from the Crunchy Grain cereal and the calories from the Super Grain cereal. We can set up an equation to solve for x:

$\frac{3}{4} \cdot 210 + 240x = 270$

Simplifying the equation:

$157.5 + 240x = 270$

$240x = 112.5$

$x = \frac{112.5}{240} = \frac{15}{32}$

Action: Answer("C")

Therefore, we can set up the following equation:
$$\frac{280}{3}(\frac{3}{4}) + 240x = 270$$

$$70 + 240x = 270$$
$$240x = 200$$
$$x = \frac{5}{6}$$
So, Jennifer adds $\frac{5}{6}$ cup of Super Grain cereal to $\frac{3}{4}$ cup of Crunchy Grain cereal to make one cup of the mixture.
The amount of Super Grain cereal in one cup of mixture is:
$$\frac{5}{6} - \frac{3}{4} = \frac{5}{6} - \frac{9}{12} = \frac{5}{6} - \frac{3}{4} = \frac{5}{6} - \frac{3}{6} = \frac{2}{6} = \frac{1}{3}$$
Answer: Answer("C")

Solving the system of equations gives x = 1/3 and y = 2/3. Therefore, the amount of Super Grain cereal in one cup of the mixture is x = 1/3 cup.

### Exam: sat-math-100 | Temperature: 6.0 | Problem 94 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: $$h=-16 t^{2}+v t+k$$The equation above gives the height $h$, in feet, of a ball $t$ seconds after it is thrown straight up with an initial speed of $v$ feet per second from a height of $k$ feet. Which of the following gives $v$ in terms of $h, t$, and $k$ ?
Choices:
  A: $v=h+k-16 t$
  B: $v=\frac{h-k+16}{t}$
  C: $v=\frac{h+k}{t}-16 t$
  D: $v=\frac{h-k}{t}+16 t$
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  The equation $h=-16 t^{2}+v t+k$ describes the height $h$ of a ball thrown straight up with an initial velocity $v$ from a height of $k$ feet at time $t$ seconds.
  To solve for $v$, we need to isolate $v$ on one side of the equation.
  
Action: 
  Rearranging the given equation, we get $v t = -16 t^{2} + h - k$
  Dividing both sides by $t$, we get $v = -16t + \frac{h-k}{t}$
  Therefore, Answer is v = (h-k)/t - 16t, which is choice C. 
  Answer("C")
Response 1:
Knowledge:
  The equation $h=-16 t^{2}+v t+k$ gives the height $h$, in feet, of a ball $t$ seconds after it is thrown straight up with an initial speed of $v$ feet per second from a height of $k$ feet.
  We need to isolate $v$.
Solution:
  Rearranging the equation, we get $v t = -16 t^{2} + h - k$
  Dividing both sides by $t$, we get $v = \frac{h-k}{t} - 16t$
  Therefore, the answer is (D) $v=\frac{h-k}{t}+16 t$. 
Action: Answer("D")
Response 2:
Knowledge: 
  The given equation relates the height $h$ of a ball at time $t$ to its initial velocity $v$ and starting height $k$.
  To solve for $v$, we need to isolate it on one side of the equation.
  We can do this by rearranging the given equation.
  We know that the derivative of the height function with respect to time is the velocity function.
  So we can also find the velocity function by taking the derivative of the height function.
  The derivative of $-16 t^{2}$ is $-32t$, and the derivative of $v t$ is $v$.
  Therefore, the velocity function is $v=-32t+v$.
  Solving for $v$, we get $v=32t$.

Action: Answer("v=32t")
Response 3:
Knowledge:
  The given equation is a formula for the height of a ball thrown straight up into the air.
  $h$ is the height of the ball at time $t$.
  $v$ is the initial velocity of the ball.
  $k$ is the initial height of the ball.
  Acceleration due to gravity is -16 feet per second squared.
  The initial velocity is the velocity of the ball at time $t=0$.
  
To solve for $v$, we need to isolate it on one side of the equation. We can do that by rearranging the given equation as follows:
$$h=k+v t-16 t^{2}$$
Adding $16t^2$ to both sides, we get:
$$h+16 t^{2}=k+v t$$
Subtracting $k$ from both sides, we get:
$$h-k+16 t^{2}=v t$$
Finally, dividing both sides by $t$, we get:
$$v=\frac{h-k}{t}+16t$$

Action: Answer("D")

\end{align*}
Simplify the expression:
\begin{align*}

v &= \frac{h}{t}-\frac{k}{t}+16\\
\end{align*}

  $$h+16t=-16t^{2}+t(v+16)+k$$

  $$v=\frac{h+16t-k}{t}+16$$
  Therefore, the answer is (after simplification):
  $$v=\frac{h-k}{t}+16$$
  So the correct answer is (D).

  To find the slope of a line given in the form $Ax+By=C$, solve for $y$ to get $y=-\frac{A}{B}x+\frac{C}{B}$.

Checking each option:
  A: The slope of this line is $-\frac{3}{2}$, which is the negative reciprocal of $\frac{2}{3}$. Therefore, this line is perpendicular to the given line.
  B: The slope of this line is $-\frac{3}{4}$, which is not the negative reciprocal of $\frac{2}{3}$. Therefore, this line is not perpendicular to the given line.
  C: The slope of this line is $-\frac{1}{2}$, which is not the negative reciprocal of $\frac{2}{3}$. Therefore, this line is not perpendicular to the given line.
  D: The slope of this line is $-\frac{1}{3}$, which is not the negative reciprocal of $\frac{2}{3}$. Therefore, this line is not perpendicular to the given line.

Question: Biologists found a new species of pale shrimp at the world's deepest undersea vent, the Beebe Vent Field. The vent is 3.1 miles below the sea's surface.Approximately how many kilometers below the sea's surface is the vent? ( 1 kilometer $\approx 0.6214$ miles)

  A: 2
  B: 3
  C: 4
  D: 5

  1 kilometer is approximately 0.6214 miles.

Action:

### Exam: sat-math-100 | Temperature: 6.0 | Problem 97 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The Downtown Business Association (DBA) in a certain city plans to increase its membership by a total of $n$ businesses per year. There were $b$ businesses in the DBA at the beginning of this year. Which function best models the total number of businesses, $y$, the DBA plans to have as members $x$ years from now?
Choices:
  A: $y=n x+b$
  B: $y=n x-b$
  C: $y=b(n)^{x}$
  D: $y=n(b)^{x}$
